<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-cb92a85ea04e8d8dc6789d22cb4da291"><strong>How to Download and Install Mod Version</strong></h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-468d558c29a03f618738567f5045ca3d">Downloading Mod APK is very easy, but you have to be careful because not every website is safe. here is a simple guide on how to download and install it on your device.</p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id8_4c69fa-ef alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-left-golden kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-8_24f24b-9e"><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Enable unknown sources: </strong>Open your Settings and navigate to Security. Enable Unknown Sources.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-8_947b3d-a5"><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Download the APK file:</strong> Download the Mini Militia APK from the link provided.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-8_7d98ff-6f"><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Use a file manager to locate APK:</strong> Once downloaded, go to your Downloads folder and tap the Install button.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-8_2321b2-5c"><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Install the APK: </strong>When you tap the APK file, your device will ask for certain permissions to install the app. Simply tap the installation button to begin the installation process.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-8_881488-cb"><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Clear data from the previous version: </strong>When your installation is complete, it&#8217;s very important to clear the data from any previous version of Mini Militia installed on your device.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-8_8119b1-30"><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><br /><strong>Launch the game: </strong>Now that everything is set up, you can launch the game from your app drawer. You can access unlocked features and powerful weapons. Now you can level u<br /></span></li>
</ul></div>
